Dapi Paipi (Dentsu News Agency)

Japanese Reports: The Japanese newspaper "Nippo" reported that Mr. Dapi Paipi, the Abyssinian envoy to Japan (honorary consul secretary), arrived in Shanghai on the French postal ship "Adus" at 10:00 am on the 10th, under the orders of Foreign Minister Hailu. He has reserved a room at the Fuxin Asia Hotel and plans to leave Shanghai on the Nagasaki Maru on the 12th. He made the following statement to Japanese reporters: Question (Japanese reporters): Is the Abyssinian-Italian dispute definitively broken? What is Abyssinia's attitude towards the League of Nations? Answer (Mr. Dapi): The League of Nations is doing its best to mediate peacefully, and for the time being, war is unlikely to break out. We only believe in the League of Nations. If war unfortunately breaks out, Britain and France may step in to stop it. Question: If the Italian army is determined to attack, will your country fight back, and to what extent have you prepared for defense? Answer: The whole nation is prepared. Question: The climates of Abyssinia and Italy are different. I heard that the Italian army's war in Abyssinia is mostly unfavorable, is that true? Answer: Not only the climate but also the terrain is unfavorable. Question: Is the climate in Abyssinia hot? Answer: It is not hot, cooler than Shanghai, because Abyssinia is very high above sea level, 15,000 feet above sea level, with a very good climate, too cool at night. Question: Every step in Abyssinia is mountainous, is it impossible to attack with cannons? Answer: It is indeed impossible. Question: Does Abyssinia have many aircraft? Answer: Not many. Question: Do you have any special mission on your trip to Japan? Answer: This trip to Japan is originally for the purpose of exchanging envoys. There are some matters to discuss. I am an honorary consul secretary and will only go as far as Osaka and will not go to Tokyo for the time being. But I have to meet Foreign Minister Hirota, but the date has not yet been scheduled. I plan to stay in Japan for a long time. Question: Japan has shown goodwill towards Abyssinia. Does Abyssinia want to strengthen economic ties with Japan? Answer: Japanese-Abyssinian economic cooperation is one of the missions of my trip.

China Islamic Preaching Society Cables the League of Nations to Mediate the Italian-Abyssinian Dispute 95

According to the Guowen News Agency, the "Humanitarian Monthly" magazine on Pubo Road in this city recently received an urgent letter from the Taiyuan China Islamic Preaching Society, stating that the society, considering the escalating tension between Italy and Abyssinia and fearing that the outbreak of war would trigger a second world war, sent a telegram to the League of Nations General Assembly in Geneva, Switzerland, yesterday to call for peace and request the League to use various just and peaceful methods to mediate the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia for the sake of world peace. The original text is as follows: "Secretary-General of the League of Nations in Geneva, Switzerland, please forward to the League of Nations General Assembly. For the sake of world peace, please make good use of various extremely just and peaceful methods to mediate the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia, and especially hope to faithfully dissuade and peacefully stop the impending war between the two countries. We have no intention, only for humanity. Mu Han Deli Lima Juntu, President of the China Islamic Preaching Society in Taiyuan, Shanxi," etc. Please call for unanimous support.

The Ministry of Finance's Ten Types of Government Bonds Were Drawn by Lots Yesterday Morning for Principal Repayment, Fifty Lots Were Drawn to Repay More Than 7.3 Million, and the 24 Treasury Bonds Will Be Paid Starting from the 20th of This Month and the End of the Month 96

Ten types of government bonds, including the Austrian Indemnity 24 Treasury Bonds, were drawn by lots yesterday morning at 10:00 am at the Hong Kong Road Bankers Association to repay the principal. More than 30 representatives from all walks of life attended. Under the chairmanship of Jiang Lufu, Director of the Government Bonds Department, a total of 50 lots were drawn, and the principal to be repaid was 7,329,000 silver dollars. For all winning bonds, the 24 Treasury Bonds will be paid starting from the 20th of this month, and the rest will be paid by the end of the month by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

Jiang Lufu, Director of the Government Bonds Department, Lin Jinyu, Monitor of the Ministry of Finance, Xu Jiyin of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Fan Jietang of the National Debt Fund Management Committee, Hu Xiqin of the Shanghai Banking Association, Yan Dayou of the Shanghai Money Dealers Association, Jin Wenyuan of the Central Bank as the lottery drawer, Zhu Qizhen of the Bank of China, Chen Mutang of the Bank of Communications, Managers He Kaojuan, Zong Boxuan, Liang Yaozong, Registrars You Dunyi, Ji Juncai, Fang Jingzhong, Clerks Wang Huaifen, Huang Qizong, Ling Qixun, Huang Meizhao, Receptionists Gong Guiqin, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, Xu Bangzheng, Ju Zhijing of the Shanghai First Special District Court, Luo Quyuan of the Chinese Securities Exchange, Luo Huizong of the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce, Jin Wenwei of Wing Hang Bank, Xu Jiali of the New China Bank, Hua Shihan of the National China Bank, and more than 30 others.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, Chairman Jiang Lufu reported, stating that today is the lottery drawing for the repayment of principal for ten types of bonds, including the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bonds. Except for the 17-Year Financial Long-Term Government Bonds, which, according to the original regulations, repays 1,115,000 yuan each time, and the lottery method must use two-digit numbers, the lottery drawing for the remaining nine types of bonds will still use two-digit numbers. As for the 14th repayment of the 17-Year Financial Short-Term Government Bonds, it does not need to be drawn by lots due to the sequential nature. Now, I will briefly report the details of each bond to everyone. (1) Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bonds, issued in 1926, with a total amount of 2.4 million yuan. It has been repaid 18 times, and this is the 19th repayment. Two lots will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 48,000 silver dollars. (2) 6% Government Bonds of 1918, with a total issuance of 45 million yuan. It has been repaid 21 times, and this is the 22nd repayment. Two lots will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 450,000 yuan. (3) 1925 Government Bonds, with a total issuance of 15 million yuan. It has been repaid 22 times, and this is the 23rd repayment. Eight lots will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 1.2 million silver dollars. (4) National Government Ministry of Finance Military Supplies Government Bonds, issued in 1928, with a total amount of 10 million yuan. It has been repaid 18 times, and this is the 19th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 101,000 silver dollars. (5) National Government Ministry of Finance Rehabilitation Short-Term Government Bonds, issued in 1928, with a total amount of 40 million yuan. It has been repaid 21 times, and this is the 22nd repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 400,000 silver dollars. (6) 1928 Financial Short-Term Bonds, with a total issuance of 30 million yuan. It has been repaid 12 times, and this is the 14th repayment. Nine lots should be drawn, but because it is sequential, there is no need to draw lots. The total repayment is 2.7 million silver dollars. (7) 1928 Financial Long-Term Government Bonds, issued in 1928, with a total amount of 45 million yuan. It has been repaid twice, and this is the 4th repayment. Twenty-five lots will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 1,115,000 silver dollars. (8) 1929 Disaster Relief Government Bonds, with a total issuance of 10 million yuan. It has been repaid 20 times, and this is the 21st repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 100,000 silver dollars. (9) 1930 Customs Revenue Government Bonds, with a total issuance of 20 million yuan. It has been repaid 18 times, and this is the 19th repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 195,000 silver dollars. (10) 1934 Customs Revenue Government Bonds, issued in 1935, with a total amount of 100 million yuan. This is the first repayment. One lot will be drawn, and the principal to be repaid is 1 million silver dollars. The payment of principal and due interest for the above-mentioned winning bonds, the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bonds, will begin on September 20-21. The payment for the remaining nine types of bonds will begin on September 30. Except for the 1934 Customs Revenue Government Bonds, which are paid by the Central Bank in various places, the remaining bonds are paid by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications in various places. Please ask the supervisors to verify the winning numbers and the lottery number book for the execution of the lottery drawing.

Winning Numbers

(2) One 6% Government Bond of 1918: No. 33. (3) Eight 1925 Government Bonds: No. 03, No. 18, No. 42, No. 4, No. 62, No. 88, No. 9, No. 97. Banks Signed Loan Agreements for Flood Relief Yesterday, Loans to be Sent to Central Bank for Collection Before the 13th 97

The 143,000 yuan in flood relief loans negotiated by the banks has been officially signed for loan agreements by the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces yesterday and sent to the Bankers Association for transfer. The details are as follows:

Signing of Loan Agreements

The flood relief loans negotiated by the Bankers Association have been resolved by the 73rd Executive Committee meeting of the Association, dividing them into two types: (A) 10,000 yuan and (B) 5,000 yuan, and sent circulars to member banks to voluntarily lend, in order to raise 200,000 yuan. As of now, only 142,000 yuan has been pledged. In order to urgently provide disaster relief, the Bankers Association sent 28 loan agreements to the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces for signing on the 6th. The Flood Relief Association has already signed all 28 loan agreements yesterday (the 10th) and returned them to the Bankers Association for distribution.

Scheduled Payment

The Bankers Association will transfer these officially signed loan agreements to the respective borrowing banks today, and according to the Flood Relief Association's reply, the Central Bank is designated as the agency for collecting these flood relief loans. Please send the amount of the loan to the Central Bank for collection before the 13th of this month, so that the Flood Relief Association can allocate it to various flood-stricken areas for urgent relief.

Interest at 7%

When the Bankers Association sent the 28 loan agreements to the Flood Relief Association, the interest rate was left blank for the Association to fill in. However, when the Flood Relief Association returned the loan agreements yesterday, it was still left blank. Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Bankers Association, inquired with the Flood Relief Association by telephone last night and learned that when the Central, China, and Communications Banks jointly provided a loan of 300,000 yuan, the interest rate was set at 7% per annum. The interest rate for the 143,000 yuan jointly loaned by the banks has also been decided to be handled in the same way. Therefore, before transferring the loan agreements to the banks today, the Bankers Association will fill in the words "7%" to inform them.

The Two-Route Union Continues Meeting Yesterday: Directors and Supervisors Elected the Day Before Yesterday; Declaration Announced at Yesterday's Closing Ceremony 101

The second session of the Two-Route Union Representatives' Assembly was held at 3:10 PM on the 9th in the Main Hall. Ninety-seven representatives signed in for attendance. Those present included Central Guidance Day Wu Lanxi, Railway Ministry Election Supervisor Han Jingyuan, Two-Route Special Party Department Instructor Li Dasan, Railway Bureau Election Supervisors Fan Shouji and Hu Jichuang, as well as all instructors and organizers from the Engineering and Construction Office, and all staff from the Assembly Secretariat. The presidium consisted of Zhao Yu, Cai Wanquan, Wu Renfu, Yao Xiaojiang, and Luo Desheng. Qi Yonghua and Li Guohua served as recorders, and Huang Rui as the master of ceremonies. After the chairman respectfully read the Premier's will, the secretariat reported on the documents received by the assembly and the review process by the representative qualification review committee. The union's constitution was then adopted, and Yang Hongyi, Lin Changgen, Zhong Ting'er, Chen Jinchuan, Qiu Yongang, Li Youheng, and six others were appointed to draft the assembly's declaration. At 9:00 PM, the election of directors and supervisors began.

Directors and Supervisors Elected

Hong Desheng, Zhao Yu, Yin Baochang, Yu Shanjiang, Wu Renfu, Yuan Qiaofu, Jiang Jiaxiang, Kuang Bingqing, Zhu Naizhang, and nine others were elected as directors. Qiu Yongang, Zhong Ting'er, Li Youheng, and Yang Hongyi were elected as alternate directors. Wang Fanglin, Qu Wenxian, Tang Ziliang, Yu Zhenzhou, and Yao Xiaojiang, nine others were elected as supervisors. Lin Changgen and Mao Panfa were elected as alternate supervisors.

Continued Discussion Yesterday Afternoon

Yesterday (the 7th) at 10:00 AM, the first meeting was held. Seventy-eight representatives attended. The presidium consisted of Zhao Yu, Wu Renfu, Hong Desheng, Cai Wanquan, Kuang Xiaojiang, and nine others. After Chairman Wu Renfu led the group in a salute, the proposals were discussed. The following proposals were passed: (1) The General Affairs Group passed seven proposals. (2) The Political Group passed eight proposals. (3) The Public Welfare Group passed nineteen proposals. (4) The Financial Affairs Group passed three proposals. (5) The Temporary Motions Group passed three proposals. The assembly's declaration was also passed. The closing ceremony was held in the afternoon.

Closing Ceremony in the Afternoon

The closing ceremony was held at 3:00 PM. The same number of representatives attended as before. Those present included Central Representative Wu Lanxi, Railway Ministry Representative Han Jingyuan, Executive Committee Members of the Two-Route Special Party Department Chen Chengshi, Li Dasan, Song Chuanji, Feng Qishu, and Wang Weixia, Secretary Xie Chengyu, Railway Bureau Deputy Director Wu Shaohui, and Director of the China Branch of the International Labor Bureau Cheng Haifeng, and more than 200 others. After Zhao Yu led the group in a salute, he delivered the closing remarks. Central Representative Wu Lanxi, Railway Ministry Representative Han Jingyuan, Executive Committee Member of the Special Party Department Wang Weixia, and Railway Bureau Deputy Director Wu Shaohui, successively delivered training speeches. Director of the China Labor Bureau Cheng Haifeng then spoke. Finally, representative Li Youheng delivered a response. Slogans were then shouted, and the ceremony concluded.

Declaration Announced

The declaration of the Second National Representatives Assembly of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Union, directly under the Ministry of Railways, states: The organization of the Beijing-Shanghai-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Union began in the sixth year of the Republic of China after the Party launched the Northern Expedition. However, the unions at that time were horizontal organizations, such as those for train operations, machinery, catering, refreshments, loading, and unloading, each acting independently without any system. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the Central People's Training Committee ordered the assignment of personnel to guide and reorganize them. In the eighteenth year, the Special Party Department of this route took over and continued the reorganization. In May of the twentieth year, the union's reorganization office was established. In September of the same year, the first national representative assembly was convened to elect directors and supervisors. Subsequently, while the registration was being processed, the "January 28th" Incident occurred, and the procedures could not be completed. Furthermore, the organization did not fully comply with current laws and regulations, and the matter was repeatedly delayed, and legal procedures were never completed. In November of last year, the Special Party Department of this route, in accordance with the Central Government's intentions and in compliance with laws and regulations, dispatched personnel to guide the entire day's management. After eight months of effort, the Second National Representatives Assembly was convened today. Recalling the founding of the union to this day, overcoming obstacles and experiencing difficulties, fortunately, both the Party and government have provided assistance, and all workers have supervised and urged each other, striving peacefully, and finally achieving success. The assembly is deeply gratified by this bright and promising future. However, future work involves numerous aspects, and the assembly has made practical decisions on the original plan. In particular, several points are revealed here as goals, and it is hoped that all workers will strive together: (1) Strengthen the organizational structure of the group. Only with healthy members can there be a healthy union. Workers must understand the meaning and application of the union, and especially need to truly recognize the relationship between themselves and the union, and cultivate the habit of group life. Under the guidance of the Chinese Kuomintang, standing at the forefront of the revolution, and being the backbone of the revolutionary movement; otherwise, if workers regard the union as irrelevant and indifferent, the power of the union will inevitably feel fragile, leading to the union becoming a ceremonial sacrifice, with only a shell remaining, the members scattered, and there will be no hope for their own liberation. Therefore, workers should regard the union as a second life and unanimously support its health. (2) Strive for production and construction. The country is facing difficult times and numerous problems. Railways are a national transportation enterprise. Workers who serve the railway are public officials of the country, sharing weal and woe, closely related. This is not only different from the distorted development of capitalism in Europe and the United States, where laborers are exploited, but also different from domestic labor-capital relations. The interests of our railway workers lie in the overall interests of the country. Striving for production and construction can only substantially improve the national economy and achieve the goal of benefiting both oneself and others. (3) Protect the interests of workers. Workers come to work on the railway and serve the country, which is also seeking a livelihood for themselves. The country treats workers without discrimination. Premier Sun has issued instructions to improve the living conditions of laborers. We ourselves see that there are still many areas where our current living conditions need to be improved. Legal demands are permitted by the national government. Forcibly seizing small gains is not what we desire, and cutting flesh to mend sores should be avoided. We should strive for self-help. The protection of workers' interests has always been the focus of railway authorities, and the union should apply on behalf of workers for legitimate and reasonable appeals. (4) Conduct welfare undertakings. The purpose of the union is to seek the interests of workers. Various welfare undertakings will be gradually established to the extent of available manpower and financial resources. The union's constitution and regulations stipulate: 1. Investigating and surveying the living conditions of members. 2. Representing workers in making suggestions and requests to railway authorities and higher-level agencies. 3. Establishing worker life insurance organizations. 4. Organizing worker literacy night schools, worker children's schools, and other labor education. 5. Establishing libraries and newspaper reading rooms. 6. Printing publications. 7. Organizing various cooperative societies such as production, consumption, purchasing, credit, and housing. 8. Holding various lectures, research conferences, and fellowship meetings. 9. Providing clubhouses and other entertainment facilities. 10. Establishing sports fields. 11. Providing relief for unemployment, illness, and death of members. These are the major welfare projects. Although they cannot be achieved immediately, they must be weighed according to urgency and gradually implemented. It is hoped that all workers will pool their wisdom and efforts to achieve them together. (5) Promote the Three Principles of the People. The way out for the Chinese nation requires the practical implementation of the Three Principles of the People. We must unite under the theories and strategies of the Three Principles of the People with the spirit of saving the country and the people, in order to achieve the independent survival of the entire nation, build the political order of the entire nation, and develop the economic undertakings of the entire nation, striving forward and never changing. The Communist Party and all counter-revolutionary forces are absolutely not allowed to have any room for activity on this route. This is the common responsibility of all our workers. Although this assembly has only lasted for a few days, the above-mentioned key points and principles have been established. It is hoped that all our workers will work together to achieve them. This declaration is hereby made.

Shanghai National Medicine Branch Association Board of Directors Established; Opening Ceremony Held Last Sunday 103

The Shanghai National Medicine Branch Association Board of Directors, since Shen Zhongfang was appointed by the Central National Medicine Museum as chairman, Chu Rongchuan, Yu Zhongqi, Cai Jiping, and Ye Chunqiao as standing directors, and Lu Zhenqing, Xie Liheng, Bao Chengliang, Tu Shichu, Shen Qiangfu, Jin Guoli, Xu Zisheng, and thirty others as directors, Chairman Shen has selected September 8th (Sunday) to hold the inauguration ceremony at the Hong Kong Road Bankers Association. The Central National Medicine Museum specially requested the Shanghai City Party Committee member Tao Baichuan to attend and supervise the oath-taking. Twenty-eight directors attended on that day, and Director Xia, Deputy Directors Ding and Gu were also present. Chairman Shen presided over the meeting, and Wu Jingqing served as the recorder. The meeting began at 3:00 PM. After the formalities, (1) The chairman delivered an opening speech, saying that today is the day of the establishment of the board of directors of the branch association. It is an honor to have everyone present to provide guidance. Since the establishment of this branch association, it has been suspended for several years due to various reasons. This association has also been suspended accordingly. Now that it has been ordered to resume, this association is also revived at the same time, and the prosperous scene is like the sun rising in the sky. However, at the beginning of development, it is not easy to set things up. This association must use all its strength to strive, without complacency, without fear of difficulties, and take a unique path to create a place of excellence. Remembering that our national medicine is profound and mysterious, reaching the extreme. Those who are not talented and ambitious cannot exhaust its source and end. Since ancient times, there have been sages, but today, our national medicine is facing a precarious situation, with a danger of imminent collapse. Letting the Yanhuang unique knowledge decline, this association is anxious day and night, thinking about how to remedy it. In terms of medicine, the gains and losses, reforms and innovations, are each handled as appropriate, but not deviating from the path of impartiality. All comrades in the medical and pharmaceutical fields should be mindful of the friendship of being in the same boat and not be conceited. Do not allow each to express opinions and try to remedy things partially. For medicine, improve it at any time, vigorously promote it, and do not be lazy or wasteful. We know that the future of national medicine and pharmaceuticals will have a solemn and brilliant day. Isn't there a great hope? Comrades in the medical and pharmaceutical fields, let us work together. (2) All directors took the oath of office. (3) Central National Medicine Museum Representative Tao Baichuan gave a training speech, stating that national medicine and pharmaceuticals have now reached a critical period. If we want to reverse this misfortune, in addition to everyone working together, we must also adopt the spirit of science. The spirit of science is to seek the truth. We should explore true knowledge and insights, investigate things and extend knowledge, and should not think that we have inherited clothing and follow old ways, making our national medicine and pharmaceuticals, which have lasted for many years, gradually lose their authenticity. Now the central government pays great attention to national medicine and pharmaceuticals, and the directors who are inaugurated today are the elites of the national medicine and pharmaceutical fields. It is hoped that everyone will instill new knowledge with the spirit of science, cultivate new talents, and carry forward the unique essence of our country. This is a bit of my opinion to everyone. (4) Director Xia and Deputy Director Ding gave speeches (brief). (5) The chairman gave a reply. (6) Photography. (7) Adjournment. The first meeting of the board of directors was then held, and the resolutions are recorded below: (1) Director Xia requested a review of the budget for the 24th year. Resolution: After the budget for the 14th year is mimeographed and distributed to the directors for detailed review, it will be submitted to the previous board of directors for a public decision. (2) The Standing Committee of the Board of Directors proposed how to plan for the regular and temporary expenses of the branch association. Resolution: Passed as is. Handed over to the Standing Committee of the Board of Directors to organize the text. (3) The Standing Committee of the Board of Directors proposed to set up a National Medical Society as ordered. Resolution: Handed over to the Standing Committee of the Board of Directors to formulate specific measures before submitting it to the meeting for discussion again. (Note) Chairman Shen donated 3,000 yuan on the spot for start-up costs, and preparations will begin as soon as the regular expenses are raised. (4) The Standing Committee of the Board of Directors proposed specific measures for the branch association to appraise cases sent to the court for litigation, so as to handle them carefully. Resolution: Passed as is. Submitted to the Central National Medicine Museum for record, and sent to the National Medicine Branch Association for reference.

Representatives of Refugees from Belgium Plead with the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau to Seek Ways to Provide Relief to Maintain Livelihoods; Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau has Telegraphed the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for Instructions 104

After eleven refugees from Belgium, including Lin Dipu, arrived in Shanghai, they were taken care of by the Municipal Public Security Bureau and temporarily resided at the Dongfang Hotel in Xiaodongmen. It is learned that among the refugees returning this time, there are two students, Liu Weifan and Jiang Gujie, who took a train to Beijing yesterday morning, so those remaining in Shanghai numbered only twenty-nine. The refugees, having been away from their homeland for many years, feel very unfamiliar with all business information. Now that they have returned from a foreign country, they have suddenly encountered the pain of unemployment. Therefore, they sent the spokesperson Yao Dipu to plead with the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau, requesting that they seek ways to provide relief. The Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau, considering this matter to be of great importance, telegraphed the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission in Nanjing for instructions and sent Liu Zhuchu and Hou Can to the Dongfang Hotel to comfort them and handle registration procedures. According to Liu Zhuchu, who spoke to the reporter of the Industrial Society, the number of refugees returning to the country this time is large, and the Overseas Chinese Village is limited in the number of people it can accommodate, so they can only be temporarily sent back to their hometowns and notified after a solution is found. Regarding relief, the bureau will handle it jointly with the Public Security Bureau. It is reported that the refugees' temporary meals are still unsettled, and it is urgently hoped that the authorities will provide relief quickly.

Guangzhou Bank Shanghai Branch Liquidation News; Emergency Meeting of the Olympic Fellow Countrymen Association 106

The Guangzhou Bank Shanghai Branch received a telegram from the Hong Kong head office the other day, deciding to liquidate, and hired British lawyer Harwart to handle the liquidation. The Yueqiao in Shanghai, mostly from the same hometown, because the branch is a member of the Bankers Association and had previously registered with our staff affairs department, in order to protect the legal rights and interests of depositors and avoid innocent people from being implicated, the Guangdong Fellow Countrymen Association in Shanghai, the Guangzhou Zhao Guild Hall, and the Yueqiao Commercial Federation jointly telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the Shanghai government, requesting them to quickly seek ways to maintain the legal rights and interests of Chinese creditors, and telegraphed the Hong Kong Chamber of Commerce to penalize the handling. Shanghai Municipal Council August Industrial Accident Report 107

The Shanghai Municipal Council reported that there were a total of 220 industrial accidents within the concession in August, with eight deaths and nine women injured. The causes were generally clear in 94 cases, and known only after investigation in 126 cases. In terms of industrial categories, there were 65 accidents in the machinery and metal industry (1 death), 32 in the construction industry (2 deaths), 30 in the textile industry (no deaths), 20 in the transportation industry (2 deaths), 14 in the printing industry (1 death), and 5 in public utilities (2 deaths). In terms of the causes of accidents, there were 8 cases of electric shock, with 3 deaths; 41 cases involving electrically powered machinery, with 1 death; 10 cases of burns, with 1 death; 1 death due to suffocation; 23 injuries due to being hit by falling objects, with 1 death; and 42 injuries due to falling from heights, with 2 deaths.

Rickshaw pullers holding licenses numbered 3500 to 4000 should complete the registration procedures quickly within the time period from September 11 to 14. From September 15, all rickshaw pullers holding licenses above number 16000 should wear the issued armband between their wrists and carry their official licenses with photos on them. Notice.

Liu Asi Exposed for Using Counterfeit Subsidiary Currency; Thirty-Two Tickets Found in the Partition Wall 111

Liu Asi (also known as Wang Asi) from the north held a counterfeit two-jiao subsidiary currency note from the Central Bank the other day and bought a bowl of wonton soup from a stall vendor in front of No. 43 Lanwei Ai Road in the French Concession, worth 40 wen, and asked the stall vendor to give him change with the counterfeit note. The stall vendor did not know it was counterfeit and gave him 64 copper coins. After going to another stall, he went to a shop to buy something, and found that the note was fake. The next day, Liu continued to use the same counterfeit note, and was reported by the stall vendor and arrested. He was taken to the police station, and two counterfeit Central Bank subsidiary currency notes and two counterfeit tickets from the Shennan Bank worth one yuan were found on his person. His fingerprints were also examined, and it was found that he was a repeat offender. According to the confession obtained by the police chief, he was 51 years old and bought the counterfeit notes from Zhang Haiqing, who lived on the upper floor of the cross-street building at No. 160 Haichao Road outside the Dananmen, paying eight jiao for sixteen counterfeit notes. The police officer Wang Yucheng was dispatched to Haichao Road No. 164 to make the arrest, but Zhang had already left. Later, twenty-two counterfeit Central Bank two-jiao currency notes (all new notes) were found in the partition wall of the cross-street building and brought back to the police station for further investigation.

Post Office Robbery Case: Police Actively Pursuing the Culprits; Patrol Teams Dispatched for Strict Inspection; Post Office Resolves to Transport Funds as Usual with Enhanced Security; Banks and Money Shops Enhance Security Measures 112

According to Dagong News Agency, the robbery of a huge sum of 91,900 yuan from the Shanghai Postal Administration the day before yesterday morning shocked the entire Shanghai. A Dagong News Agency reporter learned yesterday morning that the police authorities in Shanghai and the concessions are paying close attention to this matter and have already begun investigations. At the same time, the Deputy Postmaster-General Tao Gongchen also visited Cai Jingjun, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, yesterday to request a thorough investigation. The bureau will strengthen security at the post office. The banks and money shops in the public concession, learning from the previous incident, have also increased security forces and tightened precautions starting yesterday. The details are as follows:

Banks and Money Shops Intensify Security Last Night and Today

Since the post office robbery, the banking and financial industries in the city have been on alert. With the Mid-Autumn Festival approaching and financial transactions becoming more frequent, the need to increase security has become even more apparent. Therefore, starting yesterday, additional police officers were dispatched to guard key areas and enhance security at banks on the Bund in the public concession, including the Central Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Mercantile Bank, HSBC, American International Assurance (AIA), Bank of Taiwan, Yokohama Specie Bank, Banque Belge pour l'Etranger, Citibank, and the preparation vaults of the Zhongnan Bank and the Four Banks on Sichuan Road, as well as various money shops like Fuyuan on Ningbo Road, and various branches of Shanghai Bank, Guohua Bank, Xinhua Bank, Shanghai City Bank, Hengli Bank, Dazhong Bank, Bank of China, Farmers and Workers Bank of China, and the Four Provinces Farmers Bank. This is to prevent any unforeseen circumstances.

Post Office Transports Funds as Usual Yesterday Morning

Despite the robbery, the post office transported funds as usual yesterday morning. This is a necessary public service and should not be abandoned for fear of choking. However, security has been increased. The Public Security Bureau originally planned to station two squads of police officers at the post office, each with nine men, totaling eighteen, led by one inspector and two sergeants. They are now paying special attention. The Public Security Bureau has decided to add more police officers to guard the bureau. The concession police have also dispatched additional officers to guard outside the post office and in the vicinity to prevent the recurrence of such unfortunate events. At the same time, the post office is said to have made the fund transport procedures even more thorough.

Deputy Postmaster General Visits Cai to Urge Arrest of Thieves

At 2:00 PM yesterday, the Postal Administration dispatched Deputy Postmaster-General Tao Gongchen and Postal Inspector Huang Shihua to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to visit Director Cai Jingjun, requesting a thorough investigation and the early capture of the fleeing bandits to solve the case as soon as possible. As Cai was busy with important matters, the Secretary-General Su Liping received them. Tao Gongchen reported the circumstances of the robbery and the true appearance of the bandits. Su promised to order his subordinates to rigorously pursue the arrest and ensure a quick resolution of the case.

Public Security Bureau to Increase Security

Yesterday, a reporter from Dagong News Agency visited Su Liping, Secretary of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to inquire about his views on the postal administration robbery case. Su stated that the security at the post office was the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau, which had stationed one police officer, two sergeants, and over ten police officers inside the bureau for daily security. The area outside the bureau was under the jurisdiction of the concession authorities, so the investigation and arrest were quite complicated. The Public Security Bureau is paying close attention to the case and has ordered the investigation team of the Inspection Department and the police stations in each district to be fully vigilant to ensure a quick resolution. As for the future security of the post office, additional police officers will be dispatched and strict security measures will be implemented. Employees of the bureau must have badges and wear uniforms, restricting the arbitrary entry and exit of other personnel to prevent the recurrence of similar incidents.

Injured Bodyguards Still in Critical Condition

Of the three bodyguards and one senior clerk injured in the robbery, Lü Ruilin and Yuan Bingshu have died. Zhou Yucheng is still being treated at Tongren Hospital. According to the hospital's examination yesterday morning, his injuries have slightly improved, but he is still unable to speak. News last night indicated that Zhou's temperature was 101 degrees and his pulse was 147 beats per minute. His stomach injuries are severe, and recovery is unlikely. The public concession also organized patrol teams yesterday to patrol various districts of the concession. Anyone with suspicious behavior will be searched immediately.

Five Suspects Detained in Huazhuang

News from the Post Office last night stated that after the robbery, reports were sent to various counties near Shanghai. Local public security authorities immediately began investigations. It is said that five suspects have been detained near Xinzhuang, Songjiang County. As no conclusive evidence has been found, they are still under strict investigation.

Talks from a Certain Police Expert

According to another source, our reporter made a special trip to visit a certain gentleman who has long been in the police force and has rich investigative experience, asking about the circumstances of the case and how to investigate it. He replied as follows (the following are the gentleman's words): This case is rare in Shanghai, but it is common in Europe and the United States. However, according to my personal perspective, after review, the bandits must have received considerable training. Their grand plan and meticulous prior arrangements will be understood by anyone with a little detective knowledge. The bandits' careful consideration and thorough investigation beforehand could not have been done without considerable time. The most noteworthy aspect of this case is that the firearms used by the bandits numbered six or seven, all of which were of the same type. This is not something that ordinary bandits can accomplish. Furthermore, based on the habits of ordinary bandits during robberies, their purpose is usually only money. They have no deep-seated grudges against the victims, so they are never willing to shoot people unless absolutely necessary. In superstitious terms, bandits consider harming the victims an absolute taboo. Examining the circumstances of this robbery, when the senior clerk Yuan Bingshu saw the two bandits approaching, he simply turned to avoid them, but one of the bandits suddenly opened fire. At that time, the two bandits were close, and Yuan could not have escaped with a simple wave of the hand. As for the two guards, Lü Ruilin and Zhou Yucheng, when they heard the gunfire, they saw the two bandits fleeing with the loot and wanted to draw their guns to pursue them. However, the two accomplices ambushing beside the silver transport vehicle fired two shots simultaneously, and Lü and Zhou were killed and injured at the same time. If they were ordinary bandits, they could have disarmed Lü and Zhou, driven them into a corner, and then escaped leisurely. Why did they have to kill Yuan and Lü? In summary, the bandits were not only well-trained but also had a large organization.

Ministry of Communications to Provide Generous Compensation to the Deceased

Nanjing Dispatch: Regarding the postal administration robbery, the Postal General Administration has forwarded the matter to Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Communications. The Postal General Administration has decided to provide generous compensation to the guards and staff who died in the line of duty.

Girl Falls into Prostitution; Client Reports News; Family Reunited; Gao Jinshi is Heartless; Wang Fadi Sold into Prostitution — Han Alai on the Run, Police Actively Pursuing — 113

Wang Baosheng, a native of Changxing and the business director of the Hangzhou branch of the Changxing Coal Mine, has a daughter named Fadi, 14 years old. She was betrothed to a Hang family in Meixi Town, Huzhou as a child bride. In April of this year, Wang entrusted his neighbor Gao Jinshi to send her to the Hang family. However, Gao actually brought her to Shanghai and sold her to Han Alai, a woman who runs a brothel at No. 5 Hongxingli, Beijing Road. Thus, Wang Fadi fell into a fiery pit, while her parents were completely unaware. Recently, Wang's daughter, unable to bear the suffering of her flesh trade, entrusted a client to send a letter to her parents. Wang Baosheng, after receiving the letter, learned the truth and reported the matter to the Changxing County Court, which arrested Gao Jinshi. At the same time, the court sent a letter to the Shanghai First Special District Court requesting assistance in arresting the madam Han. The Special Court approved the request, issued an arrest warrant, and sent it to the Laozha Police Station. Detective Pang Ruiqing came to arrest Han, but she was not there. Only Wang Fadi was rescued and taken back to the police station. Yesterday morning, Wang's daughter was brought to the Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police lawyer Chen Ming stated the case and requested instructions on how to handle Wang's daughter. Subsequently, Wang Baosheng surrendered himself, requesting permission to take his daughter back. Judge Qian Hongye, after reviewing the official letter from the Changxing Court, ordered that Wang Fadi be handed over to her father and ordered the police to rigorously pursue Han Alai and bring her to justice.

Apprentice Carrying Cash and Silver Dollars Robbed En Route; Apprentice Pursues Tenaciously; Three Arrested; Stolen Goods Fully Recovered 114

Yu Niusheng, the owner of the Yutai Liang Paper Shop at No. 22 Sanpailou in the city, at about 11:00 AM on the 9th, packed 600 yuan in cash and 481.85 yuan in checks, totaling 1081.85 yuan, into a paper package. He instructed his apprentice Wang Liansheng (18 years old, from Hangzhou) to take a deposit book and send it to the Guohua Bank branch at the intersection of Miniti Avenue and Rue Wagner for deposit. Wang put the checks in his pocket and held the package of cash in his hand. While passing the entrance of Yuqingli on Rue de Montauban in the French Concession, four bandits suddenly saw him, rushed up, and blocked his way. They pointed at the paper package in Wang's hand, claiming it was opium, and forcibly snatched it without explanation. They opened the package and, seeing that it contained cash, re-wrapped it and fled south in a rush. Wang chased after them, blowing his whistle and shouting "Robbery!" Wang identified the robber holding the package and chased him to the intersection of the French Avenue and West Xin Bridge. There, Officer No. 282 on guard intercepted the robber, and the stolen goods were recovered intact. However, the other three accomplices had scattered and escaped. The officer took the robber to the Grand Bell Police Station. Under interrogation, the robber confessed his name was Chen Afang, 29 years old, from Ningbo. He said that the robbery was the idea of Dan Atai (25 years old, from Shaoxing), who was still at large. Dan was waiting at the intersection of Ningbo Road and West Xin Bridge. Detective Yang then took Chen to arrest Dan and brought him back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal Court of the Second Special District. Judge Zhang Chaozuo questioned the lawyer Fei Xizhen from the police, who stated that the defendants were involved in a robbery case and that the police still needed to investigate and arrest the accomplices at large, requesting a postponement of the trial. The plaintiff, Wang Liansheng, then testified about the robbery. Chen and Dan confessed to instigating the robbery without denying it. The court ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and granted a postponement of the trial. As for the 600 yuan of stolen money, the victim was allowed to reclaim it. Furthermore, the accomplice Bao Liren (nicknamed "Little One Treasure") was also arrested yesterday morning by Detectives Chen Jiuxiang and Li Baochang and is awaiting transfer to the court today for a joint investigation.

At 3:00 PM yesterday, a runaway carriage from the French Concession Public Works Bureau, No. 5, raced west on Hua Fa Min Guo Road from the Old North Gate, running rampant. Continuous High Tides in the City Tomorrow Morning; Huangpu Bureau Announces 116

According to the Huangpu Bureau Tidal Prediction, the city will experience continuous high tides for six days starting at 11:35 AM tomorrow, lasting until the 17th, after which they will subside slightly. The highest peak will be at 11:57 AM on the 13th, reaching a height of 12 feet and 5 inches. The maritime sector is prepared, and all warehouses have been secured with gates. The details are as follows:

Prediction of Continuous High Tide Levels

According to the Huangpu Bureau's predictions, the high tide levels for the next six days are as follows: 12th (all calculations based on the time of the highest tide) 11:00 AM no record, 11:37 PM 10 feet 55 inches; 13th 11:57 AM 12 feet 5 inches, 11 feet 35 inches in the afternoon (time not specified); 14th 12:03 AM 12 feet 48 inches, 12:23 PM 11 feet 45 inches; 15th 12:49 AM 12 feet, 1:19 PM 11 feet 25 inches; 16th 1:36 AM 11 feet 5 inches, 2:06 PM 11 feet 22 inches; 17th 2:25 AM 11 feet 07 inches, 2:50 PM 10 feet 75 inches. After that, the tides will gradually recede.

Highest Tide on the Day After Tomorrow; Twelve and a Half Feet

Of the six days of high tides, the highest will occur the day after tomorrow (the 13th). One tide is predicted to start rising at 10:47 AM, reaching its peak at 11:57 AM, and reaching its highest point at 12:12 PM, with a predicted level of 12 feet 5 inches. In the afternoon, it will start rising at 10:57 PM and reach its highest point at 12:22 PM, reaching 11 feet 35 inches. It is understood that the reason is that it is the second day of the lunar month and the 16th day of the eighth month, which is the period of the spring tide, so the levels are particularly high, more severe than usual.

Warehouses Have Strengthened Precautions

It is understood that warehouses in the lowest-lying areas, such as near the Zhejiang Industrial Bank warehouse on North Suzhou Road, next to the Yong'an Department Store on Nanjing Road, the Shanghai Telephone Company Central Patrol Station on Jiangxi Road, the Four Banks Savings Society on Hankou Road and Sichuan Road, and in the French Concession, have taken precautions, so there is no risk of flooding during the high tide period.

Yesterday's Temperature Still High; Highest at 95.7 Degrees 117

The weather in the city was still hot yesterday. It was very dry and hot in the morning, reaching 82 degrees at 8:00 AM, 83.8 degrees at 9:00 AM, and 86.7 degrees at 10:00 AM. The wind direction changed from south to southeast. By 11:00 AM, the wind had turned due east, and the temperature also increased to 88 degrees. Corpse of Murdered Woman Found in Xiaohama, West Shanghai 119

The corpse of a woman was found this morning in the Xiaohama area at the south end of the Huning Road Railway in West Shanghai. A crowd of onlookers gathered. The Outer Sun Hui Bridge Police Station instructed local Bao Gu Xueyuan to report to the local court for an inspection. After receiving the report, the court appointed Prosecutor Xiao Jinying and Inspector Xuan Zhiming to go to the scene. The corpse was identified as a woman about 30 years old, with hair that had not yet been cut. She was wearing a blue foreign cloth short shirt and pants, brown thread socks, small black shoes, and resembled a woman from the Hakka region. Her forehead, temples, throat, and right chest were all stabbed with knives. The two wounds on her back were the most severe, penetrating deep into her internal organs. She had a total of five stab wounds. There was also a knife wound on the tiger's mouth of her left hand, presumably from using her hand to block the attack during the murder, resulting in the injury. It was determined that the stab wounds were fatal. The coroner completed the report. As there were no family members to identify the body, photos were taken, a coffin was purchased, and the body was prepared for burial, pending the arrest of the murderer. The corpse was murdered and dumped in the river. The river was shallow, so the body was discovered immediately. The reason for the murder is unknown, and opinions vary. The corpse was found with a strip of riding cloth tied to the lower body, suggesting that the red tide had arrived. The police station has ordered detectives to secretly investigate the murderer to bring the truth to light.

Creditor Affixes Public Notice; Two Lawyers Consider It Defamatory 120

The Lao He Tai Restaurant in the Lujiazhai area of Pudong stopped business at the end of April due to poor sales and announced its liquidation. On May 1st, it engaged lawyers Wen Huan and Shan Yinghui to handle the liquidation. In addition to publishing a notice in the newspaper, they also posted a notice on the restaurant's signboard. Unexpectedly, a creditor added another notice on the signboard, accusing the lawyers of colluding with the debtor to secretly return the restaurant's assets. After investigation, the lawyers Shan and Ying determined that the notice was posted by Zhang Jintao, the owner of the Xiangshun Fresh Meat Shop, and Ye Hengshao, the owner of the Fang Xintai Fresh Meat Shop, who were creditors of the restaurant. They believed that Zhang and Ye were intentionally defaming them and jointly filed a private prosecution with the criminal court of the local court. The case was once summoned for trial but was not concluded. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Judge Tan Zhuohong specially convened the Eleventh Court to continue the trial. The defendants Zhang Jintao and Ye Hengshao also engaged lawyers to file a counterclaim, stating that the counter-claimants were law-abiding merchants who had been groundlessly accused, causing them great mental and reputational damage. They argued that the plaintiffs knew that the counter-claimants were not involved in the case and forcibly dragged them in, thinking that merchants were afraid of trouble and that they could easily achieve their goals. They argued that the plaintiffs intentionally caused the counter-claimants to be subjected to criminal punishment and should be punished for false accusation according to law. After the judge took the stand, the first witness, Wang Chuwen, 31 years old, from Jiaxing, who worked in the Pudong Fire Brigade, testified that he did not know who posted the notice on the Lao He Tai signboard. Shan Yinghui said that on July 3rd, the plaintiffs came to the fire brigade to inquire about the truth of the notice. Wang Chuwen replied that since the notice had already identified Zhang and Ye as the perpetrators, he did not need to explain further. From this, it can be seen that the two defendants' defamation of the plaintiffs was undeniable. As for the counterclaim of false accusation, it could not be established according to law. Shan Yinghui's testimony was the same as above. Zhang Jintao and Ye Hengshao denied posting the notice. After hearing the testimony, the judge ordered the start of the debate. After the case was clarified, it was deemed concluded and scheduled for sentencing at 10:00 AM on the 17th. The defendants were returned to their original bail pending further instructions.

The Third Day of the Public Progress Congress; Lectures in the Morning, Proposals Discussed in the Afternoon 122

(Signed) Wang Zhaoming with his seal; (2) Archbishop Cai Ning read the Latin reply telegram from Cardinal Pacelli, Secretary of State of the Vatican, on behalf of Pope Pius XI, which stated in essence that the Pope was very pleased to learn that the Public Progress Congress had opened in Shanghai and especially wished it all success, hoping that it would achieve complete results and bestowing his blessing.

Three Abducted Children Discovered on the Okayama Maru; Obvious Flaws in the Actions of Two Elderly Women; The Three Children Await Court Decision This Morning 123

Recently, the Customs Water Police have frequently uncovered cases of human trafficking of women and children for export on various sea vessels. Therefore, inspections have been strictly enforced. Yesterday at 11:00 AM, as the Hong Kong-bound Songshan Maru ship of the Nisshin Company from the Pudong Lao Baidu was about to set sail, detectives Cheng Yongnian, Qu Hekui, Li Wenqi, Zhou Zenghua, and others were dispatched, along with Chen Shaoting, an investigator from the Women and Children Relief Association, to board the ship for inspection. While patrolling the steerage, they noticed two elderly women, one speaking with a Suzhou accent and the other with a Jiangbei accent, accompanied by three boys under the age of ten. The three boys were dressed uniformly in white Western-style shirts and yellow shorts, wearing rubber sneakers, resembling children from wealthy families. However, the eyes of the two elderly women shifted restlessly, looking around nervously, easily arousing the suspicion of the detectives. The detectives separated the adults from the children for interrogation. The Jiangbei elderly woman claimed the two older children were her own, while the Suzhou elderly woman claimed the youngest child was her godson. However, when the three children were questioned, they all said they did not know the two elderly women. Thus, the deception was exposed, and they were all taken to the police station. According to the Suzhou elderly woman's statement, her name was Zhang Yuan, 51 years old, and she did not know the Jiangbei elderly woman. A friend sold her the youngest child for 38 yuan to be her godson. The child arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and stayed in a hotel for two nights, planning to go to Hong Kong by ship this morning. According to the Jiangbei elderly woman's statement, her name was Zhang, 42 years old, from Huaicheng. She had worked as a servant for Xiao Ajin in a theater troupe in Changzhou for three years. Now that her employment contract has expired, she met Zhang Yuan (the first defendant) in the Suzhou theater. Yuan was willing to hire her as a servant, agreeing on a monthly salary of seven yuan, and told her to treat the two older children as her own sons. Yesterday at midnight, she followed Yuan, taking the three children on a night train, arriving in Shanghai at 5:00 AM this morning. She took the two older children by car to the Nanshi dock and then hired a boat to cross to the Pudong ship. Yuan took the youngest child by rickshaw and boarded the ship at 8:00 AM this morning, which is the truth. The detectives then interrogated the three children separately. The oldest child, named Wei Changsheng, nine years old, from Taizhou, said his father's name was Desheng, who used to be a soldier in the army and is now retired, making a living pulling a rickshaw in Suzhou. A few days ago, while playing on a bridge in Suzhou, he met the second defendant, Tang, who lured him to her house under the pretext of buying candy, and saw the first defendant, Yuan, also there. According to the second child's statement, his name was Shi Jinhai, eight years old, his father's name was Xuekang, who pulled a rickshaw for Mr. Chen, a comprador in the China Merchants Bureau, and lived at No. 6, Lane 36 of the Red Cross Society on Xieqiao. Twenty days ago, while playing outside, he met a strange man who offered to buy him watermelon, so he followed him. That night, he was taken to the train and went to Suzhou, to Yuan's house, and stayed for several days, only arriving in Shanghai this morning. According to the youngest child, named Abing, six years old, from Suzhou, when asked further, he stared blankly and could not answer. Probably due to his young age, he claimed not to know his parents' names. The police chief noted that Tang claimed to have come to Shanghai on the night train last night, while Yuan said she had been in Shanghai for two days, so he asked Yuan which hotel she was staying at. Yuan hesitated and evaded the question, claiming she had forgotten. Attempting to shirk responsibility, the police chief, seeing that the case was clear, sent officers to Xieqiao to investigate Shi's family. Only Shi's mother, Wu, was found, and she was overjoyed. A woman surnamed, a neighbor at number five, whose son had disappeared at the same time as Shi, accompanied Wu to the police station for identification. Shi recognized his biological mother and hugged her, crying loudly. Wu said her son had disappeared on the 21st of last month, and she had been searching for him for more than 20 days. She was also overjoyed and wept. The neighbor, seeing that her son was not among the three children, also fell to the ground and cried bitterly. The police chief, considering that the two kidnappers had separated family members, which was truly inhuman, decided to hand the three children over to the Relief Association for overnight care, and send them to the court for a decision this morning. The two kidnappers were also detained and will be sent to the court for questioning this morning. Meanwhile, the detectives are ordered to strictly investigate the accomplices and trace the other missing boy.

Fei Junwen Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment for Robbing the Ancestral Tablet and Obstructing the Funeral, Suspended for Two Years 124

Fei Keming, a local real estate owner, possessed assets worth two to three hundred thousand. Fei died of illness on August 4th this year. The family property was not divided, and the funeral affairs were entirely managed by the eldest son, Yusheng, leading to dissatisfaction from the second son, Junwen, resulting in the incident of robbing the ancestral tablet. Yusheng reported this to the Huishan Police Station, and Fei Junwen was detained and sent to the First Special District Court for questioning. Details of this were reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court continued the trial in the Fifth Criminal Court. Qian Xunjiu, the police lawyer, stated that since the defendant Fei Junwen was reprimanded by the court last time and ordered to be released on bail, he did not cause any obstruction during the funeral. However, his wife, Wang, reported to the police station on the 7th of this month (the day of the funeral), claiming that she was beaten and injured by the plaintiff Fei Yusheng. The police station is currently investigating. Fei Meiwen, the defendant's brother, also reported to the police station, claiming that a wooden box in the house, containing deeds and other items left by their father, had disappeared. He requested that this be recorded. In summary, these are all family disputes. However, the plaintiff now states that he does not wish to pursue the matter. But the article of indictment by the police station is Article 246, paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, the crime of obstructing a funeral, which is not subject to prosecution only upon complaint. Therefore, the police station does not agree to withdraw the complaint and requests that the law be enforced. Fei Yusheng then stated that the ancestral tablet of his late father had been handed over by his sister, Meijin, and had been mediated by relatives and friends, so he did not wish to pursue the matter further. When questioned, the defendant Fei Junwen denied taking the ancestral tablet and strongly criticized his brother for monopolizing the funeral affairs and the absurdity of the obituary. The court, seeing that the facts were clear, ordered the debate to begin. After the police lawyer and the defendant's lawyer, Xie Chuanding, argued, Judge Huang announced the verdict in court: Fei Junwen is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for obstructing the funeral, suspended for two years.

Coin Smelting Offenders Ni Runzhen and Others Sentenced to Imprisonment 125

Jiang Futian, an inspector from the French Concession Police, detectives Wang Rusong and Zhang Daorong, and officer Liu Jinrong, uncovered an illegal coin smelting operation at Lane 117, Pushi Road, on the 14th of last month. They arrested workers Yu Qijin, Ji Heshang, Xie Laichao, Li Heshang, Zhao Ajin, Liu Are, Wen Guoan, Wang Qingzhang, Zhou Shichao, Li Arong, Han Azhang, Chen Jianchu, Han Asheng, Yang Renchuan, and fourteen others at the scene. They confiscated a large number of silver bars, lead blocks, and invoices, ledgers, and miscellaneous silver used for buying silver coins from Xiang Hongda Money Shop. They also arrested Li Guoliang, the brother of the main offender Li Guoxiang (who is at large), accountant Ni Runzhen, and sixteen others in Zhabei. The main offenders Li Guoxiang, Zhao Bingzhang, and Zhang Hairong fled upon hearing the news. The police transferred the above defendants to the Second Special Court, and the prosecution was initiated based on Article 1 of the Provisional Regulations on Obstructing National Currency Politics. Judge Li Changnian held several hearings. The defendants all consistently denied smelting silver coins, claiming they bought miscellaneous silver, melted it, and sold it to the Central Bank. After the trial was declared concluded, Judge Li arrived at the First Criminal Court at 9:30 AM yesterday and ordered all the defendants to be brought to the case. He announced the verdict: Ni Runzhen and Li Guoliang, for assisting in the intention of profiting and destroying silver coins, are each sentenced to six months of imprisonment; Yu Qijin, Han Azhang, Chen Jianchu, and Han Asheng (same charge as above) are each sentenced to three months of imprisonment; Ji Heshang, Xie Laichao, Zhao Ajin, Yang Renchuan, Liu Are, Zhou Guoan, and Zhou Shichao (same charge as above) are each sentenced to three months of imprisonment, each suspended for one year; Ji Heshang, Wang Qingzhang, and Li Miaofa are found not guilty and acquitted. The silver bars, lead blocks, and other items are all confiscated as per the list.

Large-Scale Public Demonstration of Natural Fire Extinguishing Grenades Held the Day Before Yesterday; Science is Omnipotent and Benefits Humanity; A Major Transformation in Firefighting History 126

In recent years, the public has paid increasing attention to safety equipment, and firefighting has also been improving day by day. Recently, Dazhong Trading Company, located on the fifth floor of the Continental Department Store on Nanjing Road in Shanghai, has produced a new type of natural fire extinguishing grenade. It is powerful, easy to use, beautiful in design, and reasonably priced, truly a beacon of hope for the future of firefighting. Because the company is newly established, to gain the trust of all sectors, it has held public demonstrations in various cities at home and abroad. The day before yesterday at 4:00 PM, a large-scale public demonstration was held at the public sports field in Nanshi. Those who went to visit were like ten thousand people emptying their homes, and the scene was extremely enthusiastic. The performance results were also excellent, and the audience was amazed. The details of the demonstration are recorded below:

Arrangement inside the venue: At the entrance of the public sports field, a bamboo cloth banner with the words "Demonstration of Natural Fire Extinguishing Grenades Produced by Dazhong Company" was hung. Both sides of the aisle were full of slogans. In the center of the field stood a wooden shed, 12 feet wide and 14 feet high, divided into two compartments in the middle. In front of the shed were flammable materials such as firewood and kerosene. Fire extinguishing grenades were displayed inside the shed, and a purchase counter was set up. From the start of the demonstration, there was a half-price sale for two hours, entirely for promotional purposes. Therefore, those who went to purchase at that time were extremely eager.

Report on the demonstration: At 4:00 PM, the demonstration began. Wang Yuantong, the director of the company, gave a report, saying, "Thank you all for attending today. The natural fire extinguishing grenade produced by our company is a new product in China. To gain the trust of all sectors, we have held public demonstrations in various cities at home and abroad, all with remarkable results. Today, we are holding a larger-scale public demonstration to show the actual effect."

Demonstration situation: After the report, firewood and kerosene were put into the two compartments, and fires were lit simultaneously. In less than a quarter of an hour, a huge fire appeared, and thick smoke filled the sky. Then, Yuan Qirui, an employee of the company, held a grenade and threw it into the wooden shed. In less than half a minute, with a sudden sound, the fires in both compartments were extinguished simultaneously. The audience applauded like thunder, and everyone was amazed. Afterwards, another demonstration was held, which was also very effective. After the demonstration, the person in charge of the company invited all sectors to gather in the reception room and reported everything.

Manufacturing overview: According to the person in charge of the company, the natural fire extinguishing grenade was invented by the German Mr. Blanc in 1934. Through an introduction, the company signed a contract with the German factory to set up a self-manufacturing facility in China. The grenade is made of various chemical substances combined into a colorless transparent liquid, which is scientifically filled into a colorless glass bottle that is not affected by changes. The bottle is six inches high and eleven inches in circumference, shaped like an elongated circle, containing chemical liquid, weighing about one pound. The company has now begun large-scale production because all sectors are purchasing them.

Features of the grenade: The features of the natural fire extinguishing grenade: (1) "Durable": The chemical liquid inside is vacuum-sealed, so even after decades, there is no concern about drying out or becoming ineffective. (2) "Powerful": The fire extinguishing effect of the grenade is that after the grenade breaks, the chemical liquid inside turns into gas upon contact with fire. Wherever the gas reaches, the fire is immediately extinguished. Therefore, each grenade can extinguish a fire of more than 6,800 cubic feet, and the fire extinguishing time is only half a minute to fully take effect. Moreover, the more intense the fire, the more effective it is, because the more intense the fire, the higher the temperature, and the faster the chemical liquid turns into gas. (3) "Easy to use": The grenade weighs only two pounds and is very easy to carry. It takes little effort to throw, so men, women, old, and young can use it. In cities or rural areas where transportation is not very convenient, the natural fire extinguishing grenade can be used to organize a bicycle fire brigade, which is flexible and quick to take effect, and will have great benefits in firefighting. (4) "Non-toxic": The chemical liquid inside the grenade is purely for fire extinguishing purposes. It tastes slightly sour and has no toxic substances or other strong chemicals. Even when the chemical liquid turns into gas, the gas is harmless to humans and animals. (5) "Beautiful design": The grenade is very beautiful in design, small and exquisite. If it is installed indoors, it is quite elegant.

Nanchang Performance: Starting on the 10th of this month, a fire prevention movement week will be held in Nanchang, Jiangxi. The company has been invited to participate. Therefore, the company will send personnel to Nanchang in the coming days to demonstrate the fire extinguishing effect of the natural fire extinguishing grenade so that the people in the interior can also understand and facilitate purchases.

Huade Road West Prison Project to be Completed Soon 131

A West Prison was originally located on Xiamen Road in the Central District. The building was purchased by the Public Works Department from the British government many years ago. Now, the Public Works Department believes that the building is old and unusable and has built two new West Prison buildings on Huade Road to separately house male and female Western offenders. The building will soon be completed, and all prisoners from the Xiamen Road West Prison will be moved to the new building. The new West Prison on Huade Road consists of two buildings. The male prison is a five-story building, and the female prison is two stories, both constructed of steel and concrete, extremely strong. The sunlight and air equipment are also quite adequate, with heating and sanitation equipment. The male prison also has an indoor exercise ground, providing a place to exercise during rainy days. The female prison is surrounded by open space for activities. In addition to the prison cells, other facilities such as a library, autopsy room, guard room, arms storage room, visiting room, lawyer's room, medical room, photography room, and fingerprint room are all complete and well-equipped.
